=====================================================\n     5→\n     6→-- Enable pgmq extension\n     7→CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pgmq;\n     8→\n     9→-- Helper: convert agent UUID to valid replace(agent_id::text, '-', '_');\n    15→$$;\n    16→\n    17→-- Helper: create queue for an agent (idempotent)\n    18→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.create_agent_queue(agent_id uuid)\n    19→RETURNS void\n    20→LANGUAGE plpgsql\n    21→AS $$\n    22→DECLARE\n    23→  qname text := public.agent_queue_name(agent_id);\n    24→BEGIN\n    25→  -- pgmq.create is NOT idempotent — check first\n    26→  IF NOT EXISTS (\n    27→    SELECT 1 FROM pgmq.list_queues() WHERE queue_name = qname\n    28→  ) THEN\n    29→    PERFORM pgmq.create(qname);\n    30→    RAISE NOTICE 'Created queue: %', qname;\n    31→  END IF;\n    32→END;\n    33→$$;\n    34→\n    35→-- Create Chief inbox queue\n    36→SELECT pgmq.create('agent_chief');\n    37→\n    38→-- Create queues for all existing active/paused agents\n    39→DO $$\n    40→DECLARE\n    41→  r RECORD;\n    42→BEGIN\n    43→  FOR r IN SELECT id FROM agents WHERE status IN ('active', 'paused', 'deploying') LOOP\n    44→    PERFORM public.create_agent_queue(r.id);\n    45→  END LOOP;\n    46→END;\n    47→$$;\n    48→\n    49→-- Trigger: auto-create queue when agent becomes active\n    50→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.auto_create_agent_queue()\n    51→RETURNS trigger\n    52→LANGUAGE plpgsql\n    53→AS $$\n    54→BEGIN\n    55→  IF NEW.status IN ('active', 'deploying') AND (OLD IS NULL OR OLD.status NOT IN ('active', 'deploying')) THEN\n    56→    PERFORM public.create_agent_queue(NEW.id);\n    57→  END IF;\n    58→  RETURN NEW;\n    59→END;\n    60→$$;\n    61→\n    62→DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS trg_auto_create_agent_queue ON agents;\n    63→CREATE TRIGGER trg_auto_create_agent_queue\n    64→  AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OF status ON agents\n    65→  FOR EACH ROW\n    66→  EXECUTE FUNCTION public.auto_create_agent_queue();\n    67→\n    68→-- =====================================================\n    69→-- Public wrapper functions for REST API access\n    70→-- (Supabase REST can call public.pgmq_send(queue_name text, msg jsonb)\n    75→RETURNS bigint\n    76→LANGUAGE sql\n    77→AS $$\n    78→  SELECT pgmq.send(queue_name, msg);\n    79→$$;\n    80→\n    81→-- Read messages (non-blocking)\n    82→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.pgmq_read(queue_name text, vt integer DEFAULT 30, qty integer DEFAULT 1)\n    83→RETURNS SETOF pgmq.message_record\n    84→LANGUAGE sql\n    85→AS $$\n    86→  SELECT * FROM pgmq.read(queue_name, vt, qty);\n    87→$$;\n    88→\n    89→-- Read with polling (blocks up to max_poll_seconds)\n    90→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.pgmq_poll(queue_name text, vt integer DEFAULT 30, qty integer DEFAULT 1, max_poll_seconds integer DEFAULT 5)\n    91→RETURNS SETOF pgmq.message_record\n    92→LANGUAGE sql\n    93→AS $$\n    94→  SELECT * FROM pgmq.read_with_poll(queue_name, vt, qty, max_poll_seconds);\n    95→$$;\n    96→\n    97→-- Archive a message (moves to archive table, preserves audit trail)\n    98→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.pgmq_archive(queue_name text, msg_id bigint)\n    99→RETURNS boolean\n   100→LANGUAGE sql\n   101→AS $$\n   102→  SELECT pgmq.archive(queue_name, msg_id);\n   103→$$;\n   104→\n   105→-- Delete a message\n   106→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.pgmq_delete(queue_name text, msg_id bigint)\n   107→RETURNS boolean\n   108→LANGUAGE sql\n   109→AS $$\n   110→  SELECT queue_length bigint, newest_msg_age_sec integer, oldest_msg_age_sec integer, total_messages bigint)\n   116→LANGUAGE sql\n   117→AS $$\n   118→  SELECT * FROM pgmq.metrics(pgmq_metrics.queue_name);\n =====================================================\n   122→-- Atomic task claim function\n   123→-- An agent calls this to claim a task. Uses row-level locking\n   124→-- to prevent two agents from claiming the same task.\n   125→-- Returns the claimed entry row, or NULL if already claimed.\n   126→-- =====================================================\n   127→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.claim_board_task(\n   128→  p_entry_id uuid,\n   129→  p_agent_id uuid\n   130→) RETURNS public.project_board\n   131→LANGUAGE plpgsql\n   132→SECURITY DEFINER\n   133→AS $$\n   134→DECLARE\n   135→  v_entry public.project_board;\n   136→BEGIN\n   137→  -- Lock the row and check it's FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED;\n   144→\n   145→  -- If no row found, someone else already claimed it (or it doesn't exist)\n   146→  IF v_entry.id IS NULL THEN\n   147→    RETURN NULL;\n   148→  END IF;\n   149→\n   150→  -- Check that all dependencies are done\n   151→  IF v_entry.depends_on IS NOT NULL AND array_length(v_entry.depends_on, 1) > 0 THEN\n   152→    IF EXISTS (\n   153→      SELECT 1 FROM public.project_board\n   154→      WHERE id = ANY(v_entry.depends_on)\n   155→        AND status != 'done'\n   156→    ) THEN\n   157→      -- Dependencies not met — don't claim\n   158→      RETURN NULL;\n   159→    END IF;\n   160→  END IF;\n   161→\n   162→  -- Claim it\n   163→  UPDATE public.project_board\n   164→  SET status = 'claimed',\n   165→      assignee_agent_id = p_agent_id,\n   166→      claimed_at = now(),\n   167→      updated_at = now()\n   168→  WHERE id = p_entry_id\n   169→  RETURNING * INTO v_entry;\n   170→\n   171→  RETURN v_entry;\n   172→END;\n   173→$$;\n   174→\n   175→\n   176→-- =====================================================\n   177→-- updated_at trigger (reuse pattern from other tables)\n   178→-- =====================================================\n   179→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.set_updated_at()\n   180→RETURNS trigger\n   181→LANGUAGE plpgsql\n   182→AS $$\n   183→BEGIN\n   184→  NEW.updated_at = now();\n   185→  RETURN NEW;\n   186→END;\n   187→$$;\n   188→\n   189→CREATE TRIGGER trg_project_board_updated_at\n   190→  BEFORE UPDATE ON public.project_board\n   191→  FOR EACH 207→  idle_time_pct numeric(5,2) DEFAULT 0,\n   208→  utilization_pct numeric(5,2) DEFAULT 0,\n   209→\n   210→  created_at timestamptz DEFAULT now()\n   211→);\n   212→\n   213→CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF   218→CREATE POLICY \"Service role full access on agent_performance\"\n   219→  ON public.agent_performance FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);\n   220→\n   221→CREATE POLICY \"Org members can =============================================================\n   232→-- PART 5: claim_task_v2 — Atomic task claiming function\n   233→-- =============================================================\n   234→\n   235→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.claim_task_v2(\n   236→  p_org_id uuid,\n   237→  p_agent_id uuid,\n   238→  p_capabilities text[] DEFAULT '{}'\n   239→)\n   240→RETURNS SETOF public.agent_tasks_v2\n   241→LANGUAGE plpgsql\n   242→AS $$\n   243→DECLARE\n   244→  v_task public.agent_tasks_v2;\n   245→BEGIN\n   246→  -- Atomically claim the highest-priority ready task\n   247→  -- that matches agent capabilities and has resolved dependencies\n   248→  SELECT * INTO v_task\n   249→  FROM public.agent_tasks_v2 t\n   250→  WHERE t.org_id = p_org_id\n   251→    AND t.status = 'ready'\n   252→    AND t.assigned_agent_id IS NULL\n   253→    -- Capability match: task requires none, or agent has at least one\n   254→    AND (\n   255→      t.required_capabilities = '{}'\n   256→      OR t.required_capabilities && p_capabilities\n   257→    )\n   258→    -- Dependency check: all depends_on tasks must be done\n   259→    AND NOT EXISTS (\n   260→      SELECT 1\n   261→      FROM unnest(t.depends_on) AS dep_id\n   262→      JOIN public.agent_tasks_v2 dep ON dep.id = dep_id\n   263→      WHERE dep.status != 'done'\n   264→    )\n   265→  ORDER BY t.priority ASC, t.created_at ASC\n   266→  FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED\n   267→  LIMIT 1;\n   268→\n   269→  IF v_task.id IS NULL THEN\n   270→    RETURN;  -- No claimable task found\n   271→  END IF;\n   272→\n   273→  -- Claim it\n   274→  UPDATE public.agent_tasks_v2\n   275→  SET status = 'claimed',\n   276→      assigned_agent_id = p_agent_id,\n   277→      assigned_at = now(),\n   278→      updated_at = now()\n   279→  WHERE id = v_task.id;\n   280→\n   281→  -- Return the claimed task\n   282→  v_task.status := 'claimed';\n   283→  v_task.assigned_agent_id := p_agent_id;\n   284→  v_task.assigned_at := now();\n   285→  RETURN NEXT v_task;\n   286→END;\n   287→$$;\n   288→\n   289→-- =============================================================\n   290→-- PART 6: Resolve dependencies when a task completes\n   291→-- =============================================================\n   292→\n   293→CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.resolve_task_dependencies()\n   294→RETURNS TRIGGER\n   295→LANGUAGE plpgsql\n   296→AS $$\n   297→BEGIN\n   298→  -- When a task is marked done, check if it unblocks other tasks\n   299→  IF NEW.status = 'done' AND OLD.status != 'done' THEN\n   300→    UPDATE public.agent_tasks_v2\n   301→    SET status = 'ready',\n   302→        updated_at = now()\n   303→    WHERE status = 'backlog'\n   304→      AND org_id = NEW.org_id\n   305→      AND NEW.id = ANY(depends_on)\n   306→      -- Only move to ready if ALL dependencies are done\n   307→      AND NOT EXISTS (\n   308→        SELECT 1\n   309→        FROM unnest(depends_on) AS dep_id\n   310→        JOIN public.agent_tasks_v2 dep ON dep.id = dep_id\n   311→        WHERE dep.status != 'done'\n   312→          AND dep.id != NEW.id  -- Exclude the one we just completed\n   313→      );\n   314→  END IF;\n   315→  RETURN NEW;\n   316→END;\n   317→$$;\n   318→\n   319→CREATE TRIGGER trg_resolve_dependencies\n   320→  AFTER UPDATE ON public.agent_tasks_v2\n   321→  FOR EACH ROW\n   322→  WHEN (NEW.status = 'done' AND OLD.status != 'done')\n   323→  EXECUTE FUNCTION public.resolve_task_dependencies();\n   324→\n   325→-- =============================================================\n   326→-- PART 7: agent_standup view — Daily summary per agent\n   327→-- =============================================================\n   328→\n   329→CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW public.agent_standup AS\n   330→SELECT\n   331→  a.id AS agent_id,\n   332→  a.name AS agent_name,\n   333→  a.role AS agent_role,\n   334→  a.team,\n   335→  a.tier,\n   336→  a.availability,\n   337→  a.model,\n   338→\n   339→  -- Tasks completed last 24h\n   340→  (SELECT count(*)\n   341→   FROM public.agent_tasks_v2 t\n   342→   WHERE t.assigned_agent_id = a.id\n   343→     AND t.status = 'done'\n   344→     AND t.completed_at > now() - interval '24 hours'\n   345→  ) AS tasks_done_24h,\n   346→\n   347→  -- Tasks in progress\n   348→  (SELECT count(*)\n   349→   FROM public.agent_tasks_v2 t\n   350→   WHERE t.assigned_agent_id = a.id\n   351→     AND t.status IN ('claimed', 'in_progress')\n   352→  ) AS tasks_in_progress,\n   353→\n   354→  -- Tasks in backlog\n   355→  (SELECT count(*)\n   356→   FROM public.agent_tasks_v2 t\n   357→   WHERE t.assigned_agent_id = a.id\n   358→     AND t.status IN ('backlog', 'ready')\n   359→  ) AS tasks_backlog,\n   360→\n   361→  -- Blocked tasks\n   362→  (SELECT count(*)\n   363→   FROM public.agent_tasks_v2 t\n   364→   WHERE t.assigned_agent_id = a.id\n   365→     AND t.status = 'failed'\n   366→  ) AS tasks_blocked,\n   367→\n   368→  -- Pending check-ins needing approval\n   369→  (SELECT count(*)\n   370→   FROM public.agent_checkins c\n   371→   WHERE c.agent_id = a.id\n   372→     AND c.needs_approval = true\n   373→     AND c.status = 'sent'\n   374→  ) AS pending_checkins,\n   375→\n   376→  -- Last heartbeat\n   377→  h.last_seen,\n   378→  h.status AS heartbeat_status,\n   379→  h.current_task\n   380→\n   381→FROM public.agents a\n   382→LEFT JOIN public.agent_heartbeats h ON h.agent_id = a.id\n   383→WHERE a.status != 'destroyed';\n **SENSE**: Además de blackboard, ahora consulta `agent_tasks_v2` con capabilities match\n   125→  - **CLAIM**: Usa `claim_task_v2` (FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED) en vez de PATCH\n   126→  - **EXECUTE**: Respeta token budget, timeout por tarea, step count cap\n   127→  - **CHECK-IN**: Cada N tareas completadas → genera resumen → inserta en `agent_checkins`\n   128→  - **REFLECT**: Actualiza `availability`, métricas, heartbeat\n   129→  - **AUTO-PAUSE**: Si 5 idles consecutivos + tiene proyecto activo → pause + notify WhatsApp\n   130→\n   131→- [ ] **2.2** Task decomposition engine\n   132→  - Inserta en `agent_tasks_v2` como `ready`\n   137→  - Agentes las reclaman automáticamente según sus capabilities\n   138→\n   139→- [ ] **2.3** Dependency resolution automática\n   140→  - Cuando tarea se completa → check si desbloquea otras tareas\n   141→  - Tareas desbloqueadas pasan de `backlog` a `ready`\n   142→  - Detección de deadlocks con query recursiva (DAG cycle detection)\n   143→\n   144→- [ ] **2.4** Check-in engine\n   145→  - Configurable: cada N tareas, o al completar fase de proyecto\n   146→  - Genera resumen vía LLM (barato, Haiku): qué hizo, qué sigue, si necesita input\n   147→  - Si `needs_approval=true` → pausa y espera respuesta vía WhatsApp\n   148→  - Timeout configurable → fallback action (continuar, pausar, escalar)\n   149→\n   150→- [ ] **2.5** Model tiering en el event loop\n   151→  - Lee `model` de la tabla `agents` para cada agente\n   152→  - Routing decisions → Haiku (barato, rápido)\n   153→  - Task execution → el modelo configurado del agente\n   154→  - Planning/decomposition → Opus (caro, inteligente)\n   155→\n   156→---\n   157→\n   158→## FASE 3 — Bridge + Chief: Smart Orchestration\n   159→> Chief se vuelve un manager inteligente, no solo un router.\n   160→\n   161→- [ ] **3.1** Bridge: contexto de equipo en cada mensaje\n   162→  - `standup` — genera resumen de todo el equipo\n   175→\n   176→- [ ] **3.3** Chief: detección inteligente de intención\n   177→  - \"Ponlos a trabajar en X\" → `asignar_objetivo`\n   178→  - \"¿Qué están haciendo?\" → `ver_equipo`\n   179→  - ONLY if agent is offline ──\n    67→    // NEVER release a task from a live agent — it might be working on a long task.\n    68→    // Only release if the agent's heartbeat is stale (crashed, agent is alive → do NOT touch, even if it's been hours\n    85→      }\n    86→    }\n    87→\n    88→    // ── RULE 3: Release review tasks ONLY if unclaimed AND old ──\n    89→    // Don't Expire very old entries with zero access\n    69→    const staleDaysAgo = new Date(now.getTime() - STALE_DAYS * 86400000).toISOString()\n    70→    const { data: oldExpiredRows } = await supabase\n    71→      .from('agent_knowledge')\n    72→      .update({ valid_until: now.toISOString() })\n    73→      .lt('created_at', staleDaysAgo)\n    74→      .eq('access_count', 0)\n    75→      .lt('importance', 0.3)\n    76→      .is('valid_until', null)\n    77→      .select('id')\n    78→    stats.expired += (oldExpiredRows?.length || 0)\n    79→\n    80→    // 4. **Indexes:** `(org_id, status)`\n\n- **`agent_skills`** (Skills assigned to agents)\n  - `id uuid`, `agent_id uuid` (FK), `skill_name text`, `skill_config jsonb`, `enabled boolean`\n  - **Unique constraint:** `(agent_id, skill_name)`\n  - **Purpose:** Track which skills each agent has enabled (legacy, being replaced by `capabilities` in v2)\n\n- **`agent_tasks`** (Legacy task tracking)\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `agent_id uuid`, `delegated_by text`\n  - `instruction text` – What to do\n  - `status text` – 'pending' | 'in_progress' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'cancelled'\n  - `result jsonb`, `error text`\n  - `created_at, started_at, completed_at`\n  - **Note:** Being superseded by `agent_tasks_v2` (migration 079)\n\n- **`agent_messages`** (Inter-agent communication log)\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `from_agent_id uuid`, `to_agent_id uuid`, `task_id uuid`\n  - `role text` – 'user' | 'assistant' | 'system'\n  - `content text`, `metadata jsonb`\n  - `created_at`\n  - **Purpose:** Audit trail of all agent-to-agent messages; used to build conversation history for context\n  - **Indexes:** `(task_id, created_at)`, `(org_id, created_at DESC)`\n  - **RLS:** Service role full access; org members can view\n\n- **`skill_registry`** (Global skill catalog)\n  - `id uuid`, `name text` (unique), `display_name text`, `description text`\n  - `category text`, `skill_definition text`, `requires_integrations text[]`\n  - `is_system boolean`\n  - **Purpose:** Shared skill library across all orgs (read-only for most users)\n\n---\n\n### **1.2 Activity Events & Real-time Visibility (Migration 074)**\n\n**Purpose:** Stream agent progress to Mission Control UI in real-time via Supabase Realtime.\n\n- **`agent_activity_events`**\n  - `id uuid`, `agent_id uuid`, `org_id uuid`\n  - `event_type text` – 'tool_call' | 'tool_result' | 'thinking' | 'progress' | 'agent_chat'\n  - `tool_name text` – Name of tool if applicable\n  - `content text` – Event data (max 3000 chars in event-loop.js)\n  - `metadata jsonb` – Extra context\n  - `created_at`\n  - **Auto-cleanup trigger:** Keep last 200 events per agent (older ones deleted)\n  - **Realtime:** Published to `supabase_realtime` for live Mission Control updates\n  - **Indexes:** `(agent_id, created_at DESC)`, `(org_id, created_at DESC)`\n\n---\n\n### **1.3 Projects & Phases (Migrations 075, 077)**\n\n**Purpose:** Enable multi-phase projects with agent teams, checkpoints, and iterative workflows.\n\n- **`agent_projects`**\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `name text`, `description text`\n  - `status text` – 'active' | 'paused' | 'completed' | 'failed'\n  - `owner_agent_id uuid` – Lead agent for this project\n  - `notify_whatsapp boolean` – Send updates to Chief via WhatsApp\n  - `created_at, updated_at`\n  - **Collaboration v2 additions** (from migration 077):\n    - `workflow_type text` – 'sequential' | 'collaboration' (multi-agent loops)\n    - `max_iterations int` – Max turns (default 10)\n    - `current_iteration int` – Tracking\n    - `checkpoint_every int` – Save state every N iterations\n    - `project_memory text` – Accumulated context from all phases\n    - `assigned_agents uuid[]` – Agents working on this project\n    - `success_criteria text` – How to know project is done\n  - **Realtime:** Published for Mission Control\n\n- **`agent_project_phases`**\n  - `id uuid`, `project_id uuid`, `phase_number int`, `name text`, `description text`\n  - `agent_id uuid` – Who executes (FK agents)\n  - `reviewer_agent_id uuid` – Optional reviewer (FK agents)\n  - `status text` – 'pending' | 'in_progress' | 'review' | 'approved' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'needs_input'\n  - `result text` – Phase output\n  - `feedback text` – Reviewer feedback\n  - `task_id uuid` – FK to agent_tasks if this phase spawned tasks\n  - `max_review_iterations int`, `current_review_iteration int` – Iteration tracking\n  - `created_at, completed_at`\n  - **Purpose:** Divide complex projects into sequential steps; each phase is reviewed before next starts\n\n- **`agent_project_iterations`** (Collaboration mode tracking)\n  - `id uuid`, `project_id uuid`, `iteration_number int`, `agent_id uuid`\n  - `action text` – 'produce' | 'review' | 'refine' | 'checkpoint' | 'complete'\n  - `input_summary text`, `output_summary text`, `output_full text`\n  - `duration_ms int`\n  - `created_at`\n  - **Purpose:** One row per agent turn in collaboration workflows; audit trail of back-and-forth\n\n---\n\n### **1.4 pgmq Agent Queues (Migration 076)**\n\n**Purpose:** Enable asynchronous inter-agent messaging via PostgreSQL Message Queue (pgmq extension).\n\n- **pgmq extension** – Uses PostgreSQL native message queuing\n- **Auto-queue creation** – When agent status becomes 'active' or 'deploying', a queue is created with name: `agent_{uuid with dashes replaced by underscores}`\n- **Chief inbox queue** – Special queue: `agent_chief`\n- **Public wrapper functions:**\n  - `pgmq_send(queue_name, msg)` – Send message to queue\n  - `pgmq_read(queue_name, visibility_timeout, qty)` – Non-blocking read\n  - `pgmq_poll(queue_name, vt, qty, max_poll_seconds)` – Blocking read (useful for agents waiting for work)\n  - `pgmq_archive(queue_name, msg_id)` – Move to archive\n  - `pgmq_delete(queue_name, msg_id)` – Delete message\n  - `pgmq_metrics(queue_name)` – Queue stats\n- **Current Status:** Implemented but NOT actively used for transport layer (A2A protocol takes priority). Kept for audit trail logging.\n\n---\n\n### **1.5 Blackboard System (Migration 078)**\n\n**Purpose:** Shared task board for agents to coordinate without central orchestrator; agents read/claim tasks atomically.\n\n- **`project_board`** (Central task/artifact/decision board)\n  - `id uuid`, `project_id uuid`, `org_id uuid`\n  - `entry_type text` – 'task' | 'artifact' | 'decision' | 'status' | 'blocker' | 'note'\n  - `title text`, `content jsonb` – For tasks: description; for artifacts: file refs, etc.\n  - `assignee_agent_id uuid` – Agent working on this entry\n  - `status text` – 'available' | 'claimed' | 'working' | 'review' | 'done' | 'blocked' | 'cancelled'\n  - `depends_on uuid[]` – Task dependencies (entries this task waits for)\n  - `priority int` – 0=critical, 100=low\n  - `written_by uuid`, `claimed_at`, `completed_at`\n  - **Atomic claim function:** `claim_board_task(entry_id, agent_id)` – Uses `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED` to prevent race conditions\n  - **Realtime:** Published for real-time Mission Control updates\n\n- **`agent_budgets`** (Token/cost tracking per agent)\n  - `id uuid`, `agent_id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `project_id uuid` (optional)\n  - `tokens_used bigint`, `cost_usd decimal`, `iterations_used int`\n  - `max_tokens bigint`, `max_cost_usd decimal`, `max_iterations int` – Limits\n  - `created_at, updated_at`\n  - **Unique constraint:** `(agent_id, COALESCE(project_id, '00000000...'))`\n  - **Purpose:** Prevent runaway costs; event-loop checks budget before LLM calls\n\n- **`agent_heartbeats`** (Agent health/presence)\n  - `agent_id uuid` (PK), `status text` – 'idle' | 'working' | 'busy' | 'offline'\n  - `current_task text`, `last_seen timestamptz`, `loop_iteration int`\n  - **Purpose:** Event-loop updates every tick; task-hygiene checks if agent is alive\n\n---\n\n### **1.6 Workforce v2: Tasks, Check-ins, Performance (Migration 079)**\n\n**Purpose:** Enterprise-grade task engine with dependency resolution, check-in workflows, and performance metrics.\n\n- **`agent_tasks_v2`** (Priority-based task backlog)\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `project_id uuid`, `parent_task_id uuid` (subtasks)\n  - `title text`, `description text`, `task_type text` (e.g., 'code', 'design', 'research', 'qa')\n  - `required_capabilities text[]` – What the agent needs to do this (e.g., ['code', 'ops'])\n  - `priority integer` – 0-100 (0=critical, 100=low)\n  - `story_points integer` – Size estimation\n  - `assigned_agent_id uuid`, `assigned_at timestamptz`\n  - `depends_on uuid[]` – Task IDs this depends on\n  - `status text` – 'backlog' | 'ready' | 'claimed' | 'in_progress' | 'review' | 'done' | 'failed' | 'cancelled'\n  - `progress_pct integer` – 0-100\n  - `started_at, completed_at`\n  - `result jsonb`, `error text`, `retry_count int`, `max_retries int`\n  - `tokens_used int`, `cost_usd decimal` – Per-task tracking\n  - `created_by text`, `created_at, updated_at`\n  - **Memory fields** (added in migration 081):\n    - `artifact_ids uuid[]` – References to agent_artifacts produced by this task\n    - `parent_result_summary text` – Context from parent task (populated by trigger)\n    - `review_score numeric(3,2)`, `review_iteration int`, `max_review_iterations int`\n    - `context_summary text` – Accumulated context for the agent\n  - **Atomic claim function:** `claim_task_v2(org_id, agent_id, capabilities)` – Uses `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED`; respects dependencies\n  - **Dependency trigger:** When task status → 'done', automatically move dependent tasks from 'backlog' → 'ready' + populate `context_summary` + `parent_result_summary`\n  - **Indexes:** \n    - `(org_id, priority ASC, created_at ASC)` WHERE status='ready' AND assigned_agent_id IS NULL (claim queue)\n    - `(assigned_agent_id, status)` WHERE status IN ('claimed', 'in_progress') (agent's work)\n    - `(project_id, status)`\n  - **Realtime:** Published for Mission Control\n\n- **`agent_checkins`** (Standup / approval flow)\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `agent_id uuid`, `project_id uuid`\n  - `checkin_type text` – 'standup' | 'phase_complete' | 'blocked' | 'milestone' | 'review_request'\n  - `summary text` – What the agent did\n  - `next_steps text`, `blockers text`\n  - `tasks_completed_ids uuid[]` – Which tasks were completed\n  - `needs_approval boolean` – Does human need to respond?\n  - `status text` – 'sent' | 'seen' | 'approved' | 'rejected' | 'expired'\n  - `feedback text` – Human response\n  - `responded_by uuid`, `responded_at`, `expires_at`\n  - `fallback_action text` – 'continue' | 'pause' | 'escalate' (what to do if timeout)\n  - `created_at`\n  - **Purpose:** Every N completed tasks, agent auto-generates a summary; if needs_approval=true, pauses and waits for WhatsApp response\n  - **Realtime:** Published\n\n- **`agent_performance`** (Metrics aggregated per period)\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `agent_id uuid`\n  - `period_start, period_end timestamptz`\n  - **Throughput:** `tasks_completed int`, `tasks_failed int`, `avg_completion_seconds int`\n  - **Quality:** `tasks_reworked int`, `human_escalations int`, `error_rate numeric(5,2)`\n  - **Cost:** `total_tokens bigint`, `total_cost_usd numeric(10,2)`, `cost_per_task numeric(10,2)`\n  - **Efficiency:** `idle_time_pct numeric(5,2)`, `utilization_pct numeric(5,2)`\n  - `created_at`\n  - **Unique constraint:** `(agent_id, period_start, period_end)`\n\n- **`agent_standup` view** – Live dashboard of all agents:\n  - Joins agents + agent_heartbeats\n  - Counts: tasks_done_24h, tasks_in_progress, tasks_backlog, tasks_blocked\n  - Pending check-ins needing approval\n  - Last heartbeat + current_task\n\n---\n\n### **1.7 Memory System (Migration 081)**\n\n**Purpose:** Enable agents to learn from past work, maintain semantic memory, and iterate on feedback.\n\n- **`agent_artifacts`** (Versioned work outputs)\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `task_id uuid`, `project_id uuid`\n  - `filename text`, `version int`, `artifact_type text` – 'code' | 'design' | 'research' | 'report' | 'review' | 'spec' | 'general'\n  - `content text` – Full content\n  - `content_summary text` – ~200 word summary (for prompt injection; truncated to 300 chars in event-loop)\n  - `created_by uuid`, `metadata jsonb`\n  - `created_at`\n  - **Unique constraint:** `(task_id, filename, version)`\n  - **Indexes:** `(task_id, version DESC)`, `(project_id, created_at DESC)`, `(created_by, created_at DESC)`\n  - **Realtime:** Published\n\n- **`agent_reviews`** (Structured feedback for iteration)\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `task_id uuid`, `artifact_id uuid`\n  - `reviewer_agent_id uuid` – Which agent reviewed it\n  - `score numeric(3,2)` – 0.0 to 1.0 (quality score)\n  - `passed boolean` – Did it pass review?\n  - `issues jsonb` – Array of `[{issue: \"...\", severity: \"high|medium|low\"}, ...]`\n  - `suggestions jsonb` – Array of `[{suggestion: \"...\", priority: \"high|medium|low\"}, ...]`\n  - `iteration int`, `max_iterations int` – Tracks how many review rounds\n  - `created_at`\n  - **Indexes:** `(task_id, iteration DESC)`, `(reviewer_agent_id, created_at DESC)`\n  - **Realtime:** Published\n\n- **`agent_knowledge`** (Semantic memory / lessons learned)\n  - `id uuid`, `org_id uuid`, `agent_id uuid` (null = team knowledge)\n  - `scope text` – Hierarchical: '/', '/project/X', '/agent/Y', '/team'\n  - `category text` – 'fact' | 'preference' | 'strategy' | 'lesson' | 'decision'\n  - `content text`, `importance real` – 0.0 to 1.0 (salience)\n  - `source_task_id uuid`, `source_type text` – 'task_completion', 'user_input', 'consolidation', 'review'\n  - `valid_from, valid_until timestamptz` – Temporal validity (Zep pattern); null valid_until = still valid\n  - `access_count int`, `last_accessed_at timestamptz` – Usage tracking (for decay)\n  - `created_at, updated_at`\n  - **Indexes:** `(org_id, scope)`, `(agent_id, importance DESC)` WHERE agent_id IS NOT NULL, `(org_id, valid_until)` WHERE valid_until IS NULL\n  - **Purpose:** Agents can store lessons learned; knowledge-consolidation function decays importance over time\n  - **Maintenance** (migration 081):\n    - Expire entries past `valid_until`\n    - Decay importance for stale entries (not accessed in 7+ days) → multiply by 0.95\n    - Merge near-duplicate entries (word overlap >85%)\n    - Cap per-agent knowledge to max 100 entries\n\n---\n\n## **2. EVENT LOOP (openclaw/agent-template/event-loop.js)**\n\n### **2.1 Overview**\n\nThe event loop is the **heart of each agent's autonomy**. It runs in a loop (setTimeout, not blocking), executing the SENSE→THINK→ACT→REFLECT cycle every ~10-120 seconds depending on state.\n\n**Entry point:** Imported by `a2a-server.js`; called by `openClawExecutor` when A2A requests arrive OR runs autonomously checking for work in pgmq.\n\n**Key state (global):**\n```javascript\nconst state = {\n  running: false,\n  busy: false,\n  iteration: 0,               // Loop counter\n  interval: DEFAULT_INTERVAL, // 10-120s\n  consecutiveIdles: 0,        // Track idle streaks\n  lastAction: null,\n  timer: null,                // setTimeout handle\n  budget: { tokens: 0, cost: 0, iterations: 0 },\n  maxIterations: 10000,       // Prevent infinite loops\n  agentConfig: null,          // Cached agent row (model, capabilities, tier, etc.)\n  tasksCompletedSinceCheckin: 0,\n  budgetAlertSent: false,     // 80% budget alert (reset per project)\n};\n```\n\n### **2.2 SENSE Phase**\n\n**Function:** `async sense()`\n\n**Queries in parallel:**\n1. **Inbox** – Recent messages to this agent from other agents\n   - Query: `agent_messages?to_agent_id=eq.${AGENT_ID}&created_at=gt.${since}&limit=5`\n2. **My Tasks (v2)** – Tasks assigned to me in progress\n   - Query: `agent_tasks_v2?assigned_agent_id=eq.${AGENT_ID}&status=in.(claimed,in_progress)&limit=5`\n   - Includes memory fields: `parent_result_summary`, `context_summary`, `review_iteration`\n3. **Available Tasks (v2)** – Unassigned ready tasks I could claim\n   - Query: `agent_tasks_v2?status=eq.ready&assigned_agent_id=is.null&limit=5`\n4. **My Tasks (legacy)** – Legacy project_board tasks assigned to me\n5. **Available Tasks (legacy)** – Legacy available tasks\n6. **Budget** – My current token/cost/iteration usage\n   - Query: `agent_budgets?agent_id=eq.${AGENT_ID}&limit=1`\n7. **Online agents** – Heartbeats from other agents (for coordination)\n\n**Memory context (if v2 tasks exist):**\n- Load latest artifact + summary for current task\n- Load latest review (score, passed, issues, suggestions, iteration)\n- Load agent knowledge (my + team knowledge, top 5 by importance)\n- Load pending feedback from rejected check-ins\n\n**Agent config** – Cached every 10 iterations:\n- Query: `agents?id=eq.${AGENT_ID}&select=model,capabilities,tier,team,availability,temperature,max_tokens`\n- Used to determine which tasks I can claim (capabilities matching)\n\n**Returns:** Context object with all the above\n\n### **2.3 THINK Phase**\n\n**Function:** `function think(context)`\n\n**Prompt template (sent to OpenClaw gateway):**\n```\nSYSTEM: You are an autonomous AI agent. Return ONLY a JSON object, no other text.\n\nCONTEXT:\n- Name: {AGENT_NAME}, Role: {AGENT_ROLE}\n- Capabilities: {capabilities}\n- Loop iteration: {iteration}\n- Budget: {tokens}/{max_tokens}, ${cost}/${max_cost}\n\n{DEPENDENCY CONTEXT}\n{TASK CONTEXT}\n{LAST ARTIFACT}\n{LAST REVIEW}\n{FEEDBACK FROM MANAGER}\n{KNOWLEDGE / LESSONS LEARNED}\n\nINBOX ({count}):\n- ...\n\nMY TASKS ({count}):\n- ...\n\nAVAILABLE TASKS ({count}):\n- ...\n\nONLINE AGENTS: {list}\n\nRESPOND WITH EXACTLY ONE JSON OBJECT:\n{\"action\":\"claim_task\",...}\n{\"action\":\"work_on_task\",...}\n{\"action\":\"complete_task\",...}\n{\"action\":\"request_review\",...}\n{\"action\":\"submit_review\",...}\n{\"action\":\"send_message\",...}\n{\"action\":\"ask_human\",...}\n{\"action\":\"idle\",...}\n\nRULES:\n1. If AVAILABLE TASKS exist and MY TASKS empty → claim_task\n2. If MY TASKS exist → work_on_task (use description + memory context)\n3. After significant work → request_review (if iteration < max 3)\n4. If LAST REVIEW not approved → work_on_task to fix issues, then request_review\n5. If reviewing another agent's work → submit_review\n6. If I lack a tool/permission → ask_human\n7. If I need a tool that doesn't exist → send_message to Juanse (developer)\n8. If no work → idle\n```\n\n**Execution:** Spawns Node process to run OpenClaw CLI:\n```javascript\nnode /app/dist/index.js agent \\\n  --message \"{prompt}\" \\\n  --agent \"main\" \\\n  --session-id \"event-loop\" \\\n  --timeout 120\n```\n\n**Budget accounting:** Adds estimated tokens to `state.budget.tokens` based on prompt + response size (rough estimate: 1 token per 4 chars).\n\n**Parsing:** Extracts first JSON object from response; falls back to `{\"action\":\"idle\"}` on error.\n\n### **2.4 ACT Phase**\n\n**Function:** `async act(decision)` – Not shown in excerpt but is called after THINK.\n\n**Based on action, executes:**\n\n- **claim_task** – Atomically claim a task from the queue\n  ```javascript\n  const claimed = await sbRpc('claim_task_v2', {\n    p_org_id: ORG_ID,\n    p_agent_id: AGENT_ID,\n    p_capabilities: state.agentConfig.capabilities,\n  });\n  // On success, task status → 'claimed', assigned_to me\n  ```\n\n- **work_on_task** – Execute the task using OpenClaw gateway\n  - Builds instruction with task description + dependency context\n  - Sends to gateway; processes streaming result\n  - Updates task status → 'in_progress'\n  - On completion: `status` → 'done' OR mark `error`\n\n- **complete_task** – Finalize a task\n  - Mark `status` → 'done'\n  - Record `completed_at`, `result`, `tokens_used`\n  - Triggers dependency resolution (other tasks move backlog → ready)\n  - Increment `tasksCompletedSinceCheckin`\n\n- **request_review** – Ask another agent to review my work\n  - Create artifact record\n  - Create review request (task status → 'review')\n  - Send message to reviewer agent\n\n- **submit_review** – As a reviewer, grade another agent's work\n  - Insert into `agent_reviews` with score, passed, issues, suggestions\n  - If passed, mark task done; if not, mark for rework\n\n- **send_message** – Inter-agent communication\n  - Insert into `agent_messages`\n  - If addressing Juanse, create a special instruction for him\n\n- **ask_human** – Escalate to human (via WhatsApp to Chief bridge)\n  - Post to `CALLBACK_URL` with question + priority\n  - Task status → 'needs_input'; agent waits\n\n- **idle** – No work available\n  - Increment `state.consecutiveIdles`\n  - If 5 consecutive idles + has active projects → auto-pause projects + notify Chief\n\n### **2.5 REFLECT Phase**\n\n**Updates state for next iteration:**\n\n1. **Budget checks:**\n   - If cost > 80% of max → send alert once to Chief\n   - If cost > 100% → hard stop, pause agent\n\n2. **Availability:**\n   - Update `agents.availability` based on current work\n   - Update `agent_heartbeats`: `last_seen`, `status`, `current_task`, `loop_iteration`\n\n3. **Check-in generation:**\n   - If `tasksCompletedSinceCheckin >= CHECKIN_EVERY_N_TASKS` (default 3):\n     - Generate summary via Haiku LLM (cheap)\n     - Create `agent_checkins` record\n     - If needs_approval=true, pause and wait for WhatsApp response\n\n4. **Idle tracking:**\n   - If no action taken, increment idle counter\n   - Use idle counter + idle ratio to detect stalls\n   - Auto-pause strategy: 5 consecutive idles → pause all active projects + notify\n\n5. **Interval adjustment:**\n   - Busy (found work) → sleep 10-20s\n   - Idle (nothing to do) → sleep 30-120s (exponential backoff)\n\n### **2.6 Auto-pause Mechanism**\n\n**Trigger:** `IDLE_PAUSE_THRESHOLD` (default 5) consecutive idles.\n\n**Action:**\n1. Check if agent has active projects: `agent_projects?owner_agent_id=eq.${AGENT_ID}&status=eq.active`\n2. If yes:\n   - Update all: `status` → 'paused', `updated_at` → now\n   - Send WhatsApp notification: \"Sofía paused after 5 idle ticks. Run `/pull` to resume work.\"\n3. Reset consecutive idle counter\n\n**Purpose:** Prevent agents from spinning in idle loops; force human to explicitly resume.\n\n### **2.7 Model Tiering**\n\n- **Routing decisions:** Uses agent's configured `model` (read every 10 iterations)\n- **Event loop thinking:** Uses OpenClaw gateway (which uses agent's model config)\n- **Token pricing:** Hardcoded in `MODEL_PRICING`:\n  - Opus: $45/MTok (blended)\n  - Sonnet: $9/MTok\n  - Haiku: $2.40/MTok\n- **Check-in generation:** Forces Haiku (cheap, fast) for summaries\n- **Phase planning:** Would use Opus (in future task decomposition)\n\n### **2.8 Circuit Breaker for Agent-to-Agent Messaging**\n\n**Limit:** Max 10 messages to any single agent within 5 min window.\n\n**Trigger:** If exceeded, reject further messages until window expires.\n\n**Purpose:** Prevent infinite message loops between agents.\n\n---\n\n## **3. A2A (AGENT-TO-AGENT) SERVER (openclaw/agent-template/a2a-server.js)**\n\n### **3.1 Overview**\n\n**Purpose:** Implements Google's Agent-to-Agent (A2A) protocol v0.3.0 for standardized inter-agent communication. Allows agents from different platforms to message each other using open protocol.\n\n**Port:** Railway-exposed `$PORT` (default 8080)\n\n**Serves:**\n1. **Agent Card** at `/.well-known/agent-card.json` – Metadata for discovery\n2. **A2A JSON-RPC handler** at `/a2a/jsonrpc` – Protocol endpoint\n3. **Proxy to OpenClaw gateway** – All other routes forwarded to `localhost:18789`\n\n### **3.2 Agent Card**\n\n**Response format:**\n```json\n{\n  \"name\": \"Sofía\",\n  \"description\": \"Senior UX/UI Designer\",\n  \"url\": \"https://agent-sofi-production.up.railway.app/a2a/jsonrpc\",\n  \"protocolVersion\": \"0.3.0\",\n  \"skills\": [\n    {\n      \"id\": \"general\",\n      \"name\": \"General Task Execution\",\n      \"description\": \"Execute tasks as Senior UX/UI Designer\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"capabilities\": {\n    \"streaming\": false,\n    \"pushNotifications\": false\n  },\n  \"securitySchemes\": { \"bearerAuth\": { \"type\": \"http\", \"scheme\": \"bearer\" } }\n}\n```\n\n**Discovery:** Other agents or orchestrators fetch this to learn what this agent can do.\n\n### **3.3 A2A Executor**\n\n**Implements A2A Protocol's `AgentExecutor` interface:**\n\n**Input:** A2A `requestContext` with:\n- `userMessage` – Instruction with text parts + metadata\n- `taskId` – Task ID from requester\n- `contextId` – Thread ID for conversation continuity\n\n**Flow:**\n\n1. **Extract instruction** from message parts\n2. **Log to audit trail** – Insert into `agent_messages` for permanent record\n3. **Build session key** – Use `contextId` or `a2a-{fromAgentId}` to maintain conversation context\n4. **Load conversation history** – Query recent messages + artifacts from other agent for context\n5. **Send to OpenClaw gateway** – Call `sendToGateway(messageWithContext, sessionKey)`\n   - Uses OpenClaw CLI: `node /app/dist/index.js agent --message \"...\" --session-id \"...\"`\n   - Timeout: 300s (5 min)\n   - Captures stdout (agent's response)\n6. **Publish result** via eventBus\n7. **Log outgoing response** to audit trail\n\n**Conversation history loading:**\n- Query `agent_messages` between this agent and sender\n- Last 10 messages (oldest first)\n- Also load sender's latest artifacts (3 most recent) for context\n- Build combined context string injected before instruction\n\n**Purpose:** Agents can talk to each other with full context; perfect for review workflows or escalations.\n\n### **3.4 OpenClaw CLI Integration**\n\n**Command line invocation:**\n```bash\nnode /app/dist/index.js agent \\\n  --message \"{instruction with context}\" \\\n  --agent \"main\" \\\n  --session-id \"{sessionKey}\" \\\n  --timeout 300\n```\n\n**sessionKey:** Keeps conversation context between calls; allows multi-turn conversations.\n\n**env vars needed:**\n- `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` – For LLM calls\n- `PATH` to openclaw executable\n\n---\n\n## **4. OPENCLAW BRIDGE (openclaw/bridge/server.js)**\n\n### **4.1 Purpose**\n\nActs as **gateway between Twilio WhatsApp and OpenClaw agents**. Chief (lead agent) receives WhatsApp messages, uses bridge to:\n1. Connect to OpenClaw gateway via WebSocket\n2. Send user message to main agent (Chief)\n3. Stream back response\n4. Split large responses and send via Twilio WhatsApp\n\n### **4.2 WebSocket Protocol to OpenClaw Gateway**\n\n**Connection:** WebSocket to `ws://localhost:18789` (local OpenClaw gateway).\n\n**Handshake:**\n1. Receive `connect.challenge` event with nonce\n2. Send authenticated `connect` request (uses pre-registered device keypair)\n3. Gateway confirms connection\n\n**RPC Messages:**\n- **Request:** `{\"type\":\"req\",\"id\":\"...\",\"method\":\"chat.send\",\"params\":{...}}`\n- **Response:** `{\"type\":\"res\",\"id\":\"...\",\"result\":{...}}`\n- **Events:** `{\"type\":\"event\",\"event\":\"...\",\"payload\":{...}}`\n\n### **4.3 WhatsApp Message Flow**\n\n1. **User sends message** → Twilio webhook → `/api/whatsapp/incoming`\n2. **Extract sender number + text**\n3. **Connect to OpenClaw gateway** (auto-reconnect if needed)\n4. **Send RPC:** `chat.send` with message\n5. **Stream events:** Listen for `streaming.delta` (chunks), `chat.complete`\n6. **Accumulate text** from all deltas\n7. **Split result** into 4096-char chunks (WhatsApp limit)\n8. **Send via Twilio** – One message per chunk, 500ms delay between\n9. **Handle errors** – Notify user if gateway fails\n\n### **4.4 Session Management**\n\n- **Session key:** `OPENCLAW_SESSION_KEY` (env var, default \"whatsapp\")\n- **Per-user sessions:** OpenClaw maintains separate conversation context per user\n- **Persistence:** OpenClaw (OpenClaw) stores conversation history internally\n\n### **4.5 Status Webhook**\n\n- Incoming: `/api/whatsapp/status` – Twilio reports delivery/read status\n- Logged but not acted upon (informational)\n\n---\n\n## **5. EDGE FUNCTIONS (supabase/functions/**)**\n\n### **5.1 Phase Transition (`phase-transition/index.ts`)**\n\n**Trigger:** When a project phase completes or is explicitly transitioned.\n\n**Flow:**\n1. Load project + phase description\n2. Load assigned agent + their capabilities\n3. Load previous phases' results (for context)\n4. Load all agents in org (for task distribution)\n5. **Call Haiku LLM** with prompt: decompose phase description into 3-7 concrete tasks\n6. Extract task JSON from Haiku response\n7. **Create tasks in `agent_tasks_v2`:**\n   - Map task_type → required_capabilities\n   - Set priority based on order\n   - Create dependencies (task 2 depends on task 1, etc.)\n   - Status: 'ready' (agents can claim immediately)\n8. Return task IDs\n\n**Task decomposition prompt** (to Haiku):\n```\nProyecto: {project.name}\nFase: {phase.name}\nDescripción: {phase.description}\nAgente responsable: {agent.name} ({agent.role})\nCapacidades disponibles: {capabilities}\n\nDescompón esta fase en 3-7 tareas concretas:\n{\n  \"tasks\": [\n    {\n      \"title\": \"...\",\n      \"description\": \"...\",\n      \"task_type\": \"code|design|research|qa\",\n      \"required_capabilities\": [\"...\"],\n      \"priority\": 10,\n      \"depends_on_task_index\": [0, 1]  // which previous tasks this depends on\n    },\n    ...\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n**Current state:** Implemented; used in project workflows.\n\n### **5.2 Manage Agent (`manage-agent/index.ts`)**\n\n**REST API for agent CRUD:**\n\n**GET `/manage-agent?org_id=X`** – List agents\n- Returns agents + their skills\n- Excludes 'destroyed' agents\n\n**GET `/manage-agent?agent_id=X`** – Get single agent detail\n- Returns agent + agent_skills\n\n**POST `/manage-agent`** – Create agent\n- Body: `org_id, name, role, description, soul_md, skills[], config, created_by, model, model_provider, temperature, max_tokens, parent_agent_id, team, tier, capabilities, objectives`\n- Creates agent row\n- Inserts skill rows if provided\n- Returns full agent with skills\n\n**PATCH `/manage-agent`** – Update agent\n- Body: `agent_id, updates{...}, skills[...]`\n- Updates agent properties\n- Can reassign skills\n- Returns updated agent\n\n**Called by:**\n- Frontend Agents.tsx (create, update, delete)\n- Dashboard pages\n- Admin scripts\n\n### **5.3 Blackboard (`blackboard/index.ts`)**\n\n**REST API for project board operations:**\n\n**GET `/blackboard?org_id=X&project_id=Y&entry_type=task&status=available`**\n- Filters: entry_type, status, assignee_agent_id\n- Shortcut: `available=true` → status='available' AND no assignee\n- Returns: board entries (tasks, artifacts, decisions, etc.)\n\n**POST `/blackboard`** – Write entry\n- Body: `org_id, project_id, entry_type, title, content, priority, depends_on[], assignee_agent_id`\n- Creates entry with status='available' (or 'claimed' if assignee provided)\n- Returns created entry\n\n**PATCH `/blackboard`** – Update entry\n- Action: 'claim' | 'unclaim' | 'complete' | 'block' | 'cancel' | 'update'\n- Updates status, assignee, timestamps\n- Returns updated entry\n\n**Called by:** Event loop, agents, frontend\n\n### **5.4 Daily Standup (`daily-standup/index.ts`)**\n\n**Automated team summary via WhatsApp** (triggered by pg_cron every hour).\n\n**Logic:**\n1. Get all sessions with standup enabled\n2. Filter by timezone + standup_hour (e.g., 9am local time)\n3. Query `agent_standup` view – all agents' status\n4. Query active/paused projects\n5. Query pending check-ins\n6. Format message:\n   ```\n   📋 *Standup del equipo* — {date}\n   \n   🟢 Sofía (Senior UX/UI Designer)\n      Sonnet | Design | 3 completadas | 1 en progreso | 2 pendientes\n   \n   🔴 Nando (Backend Engineer)\n      Opus | Ops | 5 completadas | 0 en progreso | 1 bloqueado\n   \n   Proyectos activos:\n   - Project X (Iteration 2/10)\n   - Project Y (Paused)\n   \n   Check-ins pendientes:\n   - Sofía: Necesito aprobación para cambiar a Opus\n   ```\n7. Send via Twilio to each user's WhatsApp\n\n**Timezone handling:** Uses `Intl.DateTimeFormat` to get current hour in user's timezone; compares to standup_hour.\n\n**Current state:** Implemented and running; sends standups daily.\n\n### **5.5 Task Hygiene (`task-hygiene/index.ts`)**\n\n**Periodic cleanup** (pg_cron every 5 min). Detects and fixes stale tasks:\n\n**Rule 1: Release claimed tasks** (ONLY if agent is offline)\n- Query claimed tasks created >10min ago\n- Check if agent is offline (heartbeat stale >10min)\n- If offline: status → 'ready', assigned_agent_id → null\n- If agent alive: leave it alone (might be starting soon)\n\n**Rule 2: Release in_progress tasks** (ONLY if agent is offline)\n- Query in_progress tasks\n- Only release if agent's heartbeat is stale\n- Never release from live agents (they might be on a long task)\n\n**Rule 3: Release review tasks** (unclaimed + old)\n- Query review tasks >60min old with no assignee\n- Move back to 'ready' (so someone else can review)\n- Don't auto-approve (too risky)\n\n**Rule 4: Promote backlog to ready** (all dependencies done)\n- Query backlog tasks where ALL depends_on are 'done'\n- Move to 'ready'\n\n**Rule 5: Unassign from offline agents**\n- Any task assigned to offline agent → release\n\n**Current state:** Implemented; ensures tasks don't get stuck.\n\n### **5.6 Agent Audit Trail (`agent-audit/index.ts`)**\n\n**Consolidated activity export** (GET `/agent-audit?org_id=X&agent_id=Y&from=ISO&to=ISO&limit=100`).\n\n**Merged timeline from:**\n1. `agent_tasks_v2` – all tasks with status, result, cost\n2. `agent_messages` – all messages sent/received\n3. `agent_activity_events` – all tool calls, progress, thinking\n4. `agent_checkins` – all standups + feedback\n5. `agent_budgets` – budget changes (if available)\n\n**Returns:** Sorted by timestamp, merged by type, with costs + tokens.\n\n**Used by:** Mission Control, audit reports, debugging.\n\n### **5.7 Knowledge Consolidation (`knowledge-consolidation/index.ts`)**\n\n**Memory maintenance job** (pg_cron every 6 hours).\n\n**Operations:**\n\n1. **Expire entries** past `valid_until` date\n   - Delete or mark as invalid\n   - Example: \"This is true until March 31 → after that, it's stale\"\n\n2. **Decay importance** of unused entries\n   - For entries not accessed in 7+ days\n   - Multiply importance by 0.95\n   - Eventually importance drops below useful threshold (0.1)\n\n3. **Merge near-duplicates**\n   - Compare all entries in org\n   - If word overlap >85%, merge into higher-importance entry\n   - Delete duplicate\n\n4. **Cap per-agent knowledge**\n   - Hard limit: 100 entries per agent\n   - If exceeded, delete lowest-importance stale entries\n   - Prevents unbounded growth\n\n**Current state:** Implemented; keeps knowledge base clean + fresh.\n\n---\n\n## **6. AGENT TEMPLATE DEPLOYMENT**\n\n### **6.1 Dockerfile**\n\n**Base image:** `ghcr.io/openclaw/openclaw:latest` (official OpenClaw runtime).\n\n**Build steps:**\n1. Install Claude Code CLI: `npm install -g @anthropic-ai/claude-code`\n2. Install system deps: git, curl, jq, openssh, ssh-client\n3. Copy OpenClaw config + workspace (SOUL.md, skills)\n4. Copy A2A server files (a2a-server.js, event-loop.js, package.json)\n5. Run `npm install` for A2A dependencies\n6. Copy pgmq.js (audit trail, not for transport)\n7. Copy startup.sh + legacy server.js\n\n**Exposed port:** 8080 (Railway public endpoint)\n\n### **6.2 Startup Script (`startup.sh`)**\n\n**Steps (in order):**\n\n1. **Inject SOUL.md** from env var `$SOUL_MD` (replaces workspace default)\n2. **Set Anthropic API key** – `export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY}`\n3. **Run OpenClaw onboard** (local mode, non-interactive)\n   - Generates keypair, sets config, creates workspace\n   - One-time only (checks for `.onboarded` marker)\n4. **Fix config** – `openclaw doctor --fix` (auto-repair common issues)\n5. **Start OpenClaw gateway** in background on **internal port 18789**\n   - Bind: LAN only (not exposed to Railway)\n   - This is where agents actually run; A2A talks to it\n6. **Clone repo in background** (if `$GITHUB_PAT` set)\n   - Clones CadenceV1.0 repo (survives redeploys)\n   - Runs `npm install --include=dev`\n7. **Start A2A server** in **foreground** on `$PORT` (Railway-exposed)\n   - `node a2a-server.js`\n   - Listens on port 8080 (or whatever Railway assigns)\n   - Proxies to gateway on 18789\n\n**Port mapping:**\n- **8080 (public):** A2A server (exposed by Railway)\n- **18789 (private):** OpenClaw gateway (localhost only, internal)\n\n### **6.3 Environment Variables (Deployment)**\n\n**Required (at runtime):**\n- `AGENT_ID` – UUID of this agent (from DB)\n- `AGENT_NAME` – Display name (e.g., \"Sofía\")\n- `AGENT_ROLE` – Role description (e.g., \"Senior UX/UI Designer\")\n- `ORG_ID` – Organization UUID (for scoping)\n- `SOUL_MD` – Agent personality + skills (injected at startup)\n- `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` – For LLM calls\n- `SUPABASE_URL` – DB endpoint\n- `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` – DB access token\n- `PORT` – Exposed port (Railway default: 8080)\n- `A2A_TOKEN` – Bearer token for A2A requests (optional)\n- `RAILWAY_PUBLIC_DOMAIN` – For agent card URL generation\n- `GITHUB_PAT` – GitHub personal access token (for repo cloning)\n\n**Optional:**\n- `EVENT_LOOP_MAX_ITERATIONS` – Max loop iterations before stop (default 10000)\n\n---\n\n## **7. JUANSE CUSTOM SETUP (openclaw-dev/)**\n\n### **7.1 Overview**\n\n**Juanse** is a special agent instance combining:\n- OpenClaw runtime (like other agents)\n- Pre-built **Claude Code CLI** integration (dev tasks)\n- Pre-built **Express server** on port 3100 (custom APIs)\n- Pre-built **TypeScript runner** (bot.ts → dist/index.js)\n- Git + GitHub CLI for repo operations\n\n**Purpose:** Senior developer agent; executes code, runs tests, interacts with repo, handles complex dev tasks.\n\n### **7.2 Dockerfile (`openclaw-dev/Dockerfile`)**\n\n**Base:** `ghcr.io/openclaw/openclaw:latest`\n\n**Additional installs:**\n- `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` (global, for code execution)\n- `gh` (GitHub CLI, for repo operations)\n\n**Build steps:**\n1. OpenClaw config + workspace\n2. Juanse pre-compiled JS: Copy package.json + dist/ (no TypeScript step)\n3. A2A server files (shared from agent-template)\n4. **NOTE:** event-loop.js is synced from agent-template (comment: \"source of truth\")\n5. npm install for Juanse + A2A deps\n\n### **7.3 Startup Script (`startup-openclaw.sh`)**\n\n**Parallel startup:** Everything in background except A2A server.\n\n**Background operations:**\n1. OpenClaw onboard\n2. Fix config\n3. **Start gateway on 18789**\n4. **Git setup:** Clone repo if missing, else `git pull`, auth with `gh`\n5. **Claude Code setup:** Write settings.json with permissions (Read, Write, Edit, Bash, Glob, Grep, WebSearch)\n6. **Juanse Express on 3100** – Custom API server (non-critical, failures ignored)\n\n**Foreground:**\n- **A2A server on `$PORT`** – Blocks; this is the main process\n\n### **7.4 Files**\n\n- **`bot.ts`** – Express router for WhatsApp commands\n  - Handles `/code <task>`, `/opus`, `/haiku`, `/pull`, `/login`, `/status`, `/auth`\n  - Delegates to `runClaudeTask()` for execution\n  - Streams progress back to WhatsApp\n  - Max 10 min per task; auto-releases stuck locks\n\n- **`claude-runner.ts`** – Runs Claude Code CLI with streaming\n  - Spawns `claude` process with task + model + max-turns\n  - Parses stream-json output (type: \"result\", \"assistant\")\n  - Sends natural language messages to WhatsApp (filters code blocks)\n  - Heartbeat every 30s if no messages (\"Still working...\")\n\n---\n\n## **8. FRONTEND INTEGRATION**\n\n### **8.1 AgentContext (`src/contexts/AgentContext.tsx`)**\n\n**Type definitions for all agent-related entities:**\n\n- **`Agent`** – Core agent type with workforce v2 fields:\n  - Basic: id, org_id, name, role, description, soul_md, status\n  - Railway: railway_service_id, railway_url\n  - Workforce: model, model_provider, temperature, max_tokens, parent_agent_id, team, tier, capabilities, objectives, availability\n\n- **`AgentTaskV2`** – Task from agent_tasks_v2:\n  - id, org_id, project_id, parent_task_id, title, description, task_type\n  - priority, story_points, required_capabilities, depends_on\n  - assigned_agent_id, assigned_at, status, progress_pct\n  - started_at, completed_at, result, error, tokens_used, cost_usd\n\n- **`AgentArtifact`** – Work output:\n  - id, org_id, task_id, project_id, filename, version, artifact_type\n  - content, content_summary, created_by, created_at\n\n- **`AgentReview`** – Feedback on artifact:\n  - id, org_id, task_id, artifact_id, reviewer_agent_id\n  - score, passed, issues[], suggestions[], iteration\n\n- **`AgentKnowledge`** – Semantic memory:\n  - id, org_id, agent_id, scope, category, content, importance\n  - access_count, valid_until, source_type\n\n- **`AgentCheckin`** – Standup/approval:\n  - id, org_id, agent_id, project_id, checkin_type, summary\n  - next_steps, blockers, needs_approval, status, feedback\n  - responded_at, expires_at, fallback_action\n\n**Hooks:** `useAgents()` – queries Supabase with TanStack Query; provides agents, tasks, artifacts, reviews, etc.\n\n### **8.2 Agents Page (`src/pages/Agents.tsx`)**\n\n**Planned redesign (from tasks/todo.md):**\n\n**Views:**\n1. **Org Chart** – Hierarchical tree (Chief → Team Leads → Workers)\n   - Visual node tree using React Flow\n   - Drag-drop to reassign reporting\n   - Each node shows: name, role, status, model, team, workload count\n\n2. **Grid Cards** – Alternative flat view\n   - Cards per agent\n   - Availability badge (green=available, blue=working, red=blocked, gray=offline)\n   - Model badge (Opus/Sonnet/Haiku)\n   - Team badge\n   - Workload count\n\n**Create Agent Modal:**\n- Name, role, description, soul_md (textarea)\n- Model selector (Opus/Sonnet/Haiku)\n- Temperature slider\n- Team dropdown\n- Parent agent dropdown (reporting to)\n- Tier (Manager/Team Lead/Worker)\n- Capabilities multi-select\n- Objectives textarea\n\n**Current state:** Basic grid view exists; org chart redesign pending.\n\n---\n\n## **9. KEY WORKFLOWS**\n\n### **9.1 Task Execution Flow**\n\n```\nUser/Admin creates task in agent_tasks_v2 (status: backlog)\n    ↓\nTask dependencies resolve → status: ready\n    ↓\nAgent (in event loop) queries available ready tasks\n    ↓\nAgent calls claim_task_v2() RPC (atomic claim)\n    ↓\nTask claimed → status: claimed, assigned_agent_id = agent\n    ↓\nAgent calls think() → decides to work_on_task\n    ↓\nAgent executes via OpenClaw gateway (streaming)\n    ↓\nAgent updates task → status: in_progress, started_at = now\n    ↓\nAgent completes work\n    ↓\nAgent updates task → status: done, completed_at = now, result = {...}\n    ↓\nTrigger fires: resolve_task_dependencies()\n    ↓\nAny tasks depending on this one → backlog to ready\n    ↓\nCheck-in counter increments; if threshold hit → generate standup\n    ↓\nIf standup needs_approval → pause and wait for WhatsApp response\n```\n\n### **9.2 Check-in Workflow**\n\n```\nAgent completes task #3 (after completing 3 tasks total)\n    ↓\nEvent-loop: tasksCompletedSinceCheckin == 3\n    ↓\nGenerate summary via Haiku LLM:\n   \"What did you do?\" → task titles + results\n   \"What's next?\" → peek at next pending task\n   \"Any blockers?\" → check if task failed\n    ↓\nInsert agent_checkins row:\n   summary = \"Completed design review, mockups approved, ready for dev\"\n   needs_approval = false (or true if blocker)\n   status = \"sent\"\n    ↓\nIf needs_approval = true:\n   Post to /api/agent-callback (WhatsApp to Chief)\n   agent pauses (doesn't claim more tasks)\n   Wait for response (timeout = expires_at + fallback_action)\n    ↓\nIf human responds (via Chief/WhatsApp):\n   Update agent_checkins.feedback = response\n   status = \"approved\" or \"rejected\"\n   Agent resumes if approved\n    ↓\nReset tasksCompletedSinceCheckin = 0\n```\n\n### **9.3 Inter-Agent Communication**\n\n```\nAgent A wants Agent B to review its work\n    ↓\nAgent A: send_message({ to_agent: \"Sofía\", message: \"Please review...\" })\n    ↓\nInsert into agent_messages:\n   from_agent_id = Agent A\n   to_agent_id = Sofía (Agent B)\n   content = \"Please review...\"\n    ↓\nAgent B's event loop: sense() fetches inbox\n    ↓\nAgent B sees message, decides to submit_review\n    ↓\nAgent B calls sendToGateway() with review task\n    ↓\nA2A server of Agent B (if A2A request):\n   Extracts instruction\n   Loads conversation history from agent_messages\n   Loads recent artifacts from Agent A\n   Sends to OpenClaw gateway with context\n    ↓\nAgent B generates review:\n   score, passed, issues[], suggestions[]\n    ↓\nInsert agent_reviews row\n    ↓\nIf passed = true: Task status → done\n   If passed = false: Task status → in_progress (for rework)\n```\n\n### **9.4 Project Phase Workflow**\n\n```\nProject created with Phase 1 description\n    ↓\nedge function phase-transition called\n    ↓\nHaiku LLM decomposes description into tasks:\n   {title, description, task_type, required_capabilities, priority, depends_on}\n    ↓\nInsert tasks into agent_tasks_v2 (status: ready)\n    ↓\nAgents claim tasks atomically\n    ↓\nAgents work on tasks\n    ↓\nWhen all phase 1 tasks are done:\n   Phase status → completed\n   next phase (Phase 2) transitions\n    ↓\nphase-transition called again for Phase 2\n    ↓\nCycle repeats until all phases done\n    ↓\nProject status → completed\n```\n\n---\n\n## **10. KNOWN ISSUES & LIMITATIONS**\n\n### **10.1 Current Blockers**\n\n1. **pgmq-consumer WebSocket rewrite (BLOCKING)**\n   - Originally planned for async inter-agent communication\n   - Requires WebSocket consumer to work with OpenClaw gateway\n   - Currently NOT in use; A2A protocol takes priority\n   - If needed: `openclaw-dev/pgmq-consumer.js` exists but needs debugging\n\n2. **Event loop SOUL.md injection**\n   - Works but requires env var `SOUL_MD` to be set at container startup\n   - No easy way to update SOUL.md without redeploy\n   - Mitigation: Store in DB + pull at startup (not yet implemented)\n\n3. **Model switching at runtime**\n   - Agent's model is cached and reloaded every 10 iterations\n   - Changing model in DB takes up to 10 iterations to take effect\n   - Not ideal for dynamic workforce management\n\n4. **Check-in timeout enforcement**\n   - Check-ins have `expires_at`, but no automated cleanup\n   - If human never responds, agent waits forever (or until timeout)\n   - Fallback action not enforced (needs cron job)\n\n### **10.2 Limitations**\n\n1. **A2A Protocol v0.3.0 is new**\n   - Only agent discovery + basic message/send implemented\n   - No streaming, no push notifications\n   - Error handling minimal\n\n2. **Budget enforcement**\n   - Soft alerts at 80% and hard stop at 100%\n   - No per-task budget limits (only per-agent)\n   - Cost model is blended (input + output averaged) – not precise\n\n3. **Memory system not fully utilized**\n   - `agent_knowledge` table exists but not heavily populated\n   - Knowledge decay/merge works but not heavily tested\n   - Agent prompts don't consistently inject knowledge context\n\n4. **Dependency resolution is basic**\n   - Simple DAG (directed acyclic graph)\n   - No cycle detection\n   - No smart task scheduling (first-in-first-out)\n\n5. **Workforce hierarchy not enforced**\n   - Parent_agent_id exists but not used to control task assignments\n   - Managers not actually managing (reviewing, escalating, reassigning)\n   - No cascading pauses/resumes through hierarchy\n\n### **10.3 Performance Considerations**\n\n1. **Event loop polling every 10-120s**\n   - Agents are not truly reactive; they check for work on interval\n   - Better approach: pgmq notifications (not yet used)\n\n2. **Supabase REST API calls in event loop**\n   - ~7 parallel queries per SENSE phase\n   - Could be optimized with custom stored procedures\n\n3. **Token pricing calculation in event-loop.js**\n   - Estimates based on character count (~1 token per 4 chars)\n   - Not accurate; should use Anthropic token counter or actual usage\n\n4. **Heartbeat updates every tick**\n   - 10K agents × every 20s = 500 RPS to `agent_heartbeats` table\n   - Needs batching or debouncing\n\n---\n\n## **11.
